// –ò–º–ø–æ—Ä—Ç—ã
import 'package:http/http.dart' as http;
import 'dart:convert' as convert;
import 'dart:async';
import 'package:just_audio/just_audio.dart';

class ElevenLabs {
static const apiKey = 'XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX';

static Future speak(String text) async {
try {
final stream = await _fetch(text);
final player = AudioPlayer();
await player.setAudioSource(_MyCustomSource(stream));
player.play();
} catch (ex) {
print('Error: $ex');
}
}

static Future<Stream<List<int>>> _fetch(String text) async {
const voiceId = '21m00Tcm4TlvDq8ikWAM';
const url =
'https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/text-to-speech/$voiceId/stream'; // –ü—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å streaming API
final request = http.Request('POST', Uri.parse(url));
request.headers.addAll({
'xi-api-key': apiKey,
'Content-Type': 'application/json',
'accept': 'audio/mpeg',
});
request.body = convert.json.encode({
"text": text,
"model_id": "eleven_multilingual_v1",
"voice_settings": {"stability": 0.2, "similarity_boost": 0.8}
});

final response = await http.Client().send(request);

if (response.statusCode != 200) {
throw Exception('Eleven Labs API Failed.');
}
return response.stream;
}
}

class _MyCustomSource extends StreamAudioSource {
final Stream<List<int>> stream;

_MyCustomSource(this.stream);

@override
Future<StreamAudioResponse> request([int? start, int? end]) async {
// We don't know the length of the stream, so we set contentLength, offset and sourceLength to null.
return StreamAudioResponse(
stream: stream,
contentType: 'audio/mpeg',
contentLength: null,
offset: null,
sourceLength: null,
);
}
}

Future<void> textToSpeak(String text) {
return ElevenLabs.speak(text);
}
